# RustRedis

- RustRedis/ - Repository root containing the Redis-like server implementation, benchmark tooling, documentation, and generated artifacts.
  - .venv/ - Python virtual environment containing interpreter binaries and installed Python packages used by benchmark tooling.
    - .gitignore - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
    - bin/ - Virtual environment executables and activation scripts for Python commands.
      - Activate.ps1 - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - activate - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - activate.csh - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - activate.fish - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - f2py - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - fonttools - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - numpy-config - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - pip - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - pip3 - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - pip3.14 - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - pyftmerge - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - pyftsubset - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - python - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - python3 - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - python3.14 - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - ttx - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
      - 𝜋thon - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.
    - include/ - C/C++ header files exposed by packages installed in the virtual environment.
    - lib/ - Library directory for the virtual environment runtime and Python package data.
      - python3.14/ - Python version-specific standard library and environment-managed modules.
        - site-packages/ - Python version-specific standard library and environment-managed modules.
          - PIL/ - Python version-specific standard library and environment-managed modules.
            - .dylibs/ - Python version-specific standard library and environment-managed modules.
              - libXau.6.dylib - Virtual environment file (package code, metadata, cache, or executable) managed automatically by Python tooling.

          - server.log - Project file supporting source code, tooling, or generated experiment outputs.
  - src/ - Primary Rust source tree for server runtime, protocol handling, persistence, and metrics.
    - bin/ - Binary entry points compiled by Cargo for runnable server targets.
      - server.rs - Dedicated server binary entry point used by Cargo binary target configuration.
    - cmd/ - Rust command parsing and command dispatch module sources.
      - mod.rs - Rust source file implementing the mod module logic.
    - command_metrics.rs - Rust source file implementing the command metrics module logic.
    - connection.rs - Rust source file implementing the connection module logic.
    - db/ - Database-specific modules and tests for in-memory data structures.
    - db.rs - Rust source file implementing the db module logic.
      - tests.rs - Database module tests validating correctness of key data operations.
    - db_dashmap.rs - Rust source file implementing the db dashmap module logic.
    - frame.rs - Rust source file implementing the frame module logic.
    - lib.rs - Library crate root exposing shared server modules and public APIs.
    - main.rs - Primary executable entry point for launching the RustRedis server application.
    - metrics.rs - Rust source file implementing the metrics module logic.
    - persistence.rs - Rust source file implementing the persistence module logic.
    - pubsub.rs - Rust source file implementing the pubsub module logic.
  - target/ - Cargo build output directory containing compiled binaries, dependencies, and intermediates.
    - .rustc_info.json - Cargo-generated build artifact or intermediate file used for compilation and linking.
    - CACHEDIR.TAG - Cargo-generated build artifact or intermediate file used for compilation and linking.
    - release/ - Release-mode build outputs, including optimized executables and compiler artifacts.
      - .cargo-lock - Cargo-generated build artifact or intermediate file used for compilation and linking.
      - .fingerprint/ - Cargo-generated build subdirectory used for artifacts and intermediate build state.
